# Text Elements
Q1 (a) State the reagents and conditions needed to convert benzene into ^ZO6B1Um0

(i) chlorobenzene, ^dCGwXXeo

(ii) bromobenzene, ^4d7QQaQw

(iii) nitrobenzene. ^t7nj83NN

(b) The nitration of benzene is a two-step reaction that can be represented as follows. ^c4KSQZno

..[4] ^Che118PE

(i) Identify the cation A+. ^NzU4orM4

(ii) Draw the structure of the intermediate B in the box. ^xAg5nIJ8

(c) The position of substitution during the electrophilic substitution of arenes is determined ^Eglb43UH

by the nature of the group already attached to the ring. ^9cLdSyOY

Electron-withdrawing groups such as -CO2H or -NO2 direct the incoming group to the ^woDjQ85B

3-position. ^ObnIpHSW

On the other hand, electron-donating groups such as -CH3 or -NH2 direct the incoming ^ODKVBzJg

group to the 2- or 4- positions. ^zHZzZyac

Use this information to suggest a likely structure for the organic product of each of the ^nyVj9IiH

following reactions. ^Zy1poBWN

(i) ^kBJVdEDi

[2] ^4q7gdCDp

(June 2004 Q5) ^DjxAVlQ6

Nitronium Ion ^LGljufce

Note
- Reactant Goes where
first and second is relevant! ^HRpBpRh7

1 ^XXSnUYFQ

(ii) ^TERyPurz
